-go against, a ku dhaggan. e.g. Over against the door. b ka soo horjeedka. e.g. A book store over against the mosque.

-over and above, ku saa'id; ku kordhid. e.g. She had some services to pay for over and above the repair of the watch.

-over and done with, dhammayn kulli.

-over and over, ku celcelin; ku noqnoqod. e.g. Read it over and over until you learn it right. over- horgale (prefix). 1 dhaafa (buux-dhaaf; tira-dhaaf). e.g. Over crowed. 2 kabaxsan caadiga. e.g. Oversize. Overtime. 3 laga dul xirto. e.g. Overcoat. 4 gudubsan ama dhaafsan. e.g. Overseas. 5 kor. e.g. Overhang. overachieve (,owvara'jiiv) v. qabatin in dheeraad ah. overage1 (‘owvrij) n. dheeraad; ka badan intii la qiyaasay.

overage2 overdo

overage2 adj. ka wayn da' la cayimay.

overall (‘owva,rool) adj. kulli ama gabi ahaan. e.g. An over all increase of 5 percent. The overall peace negotiation is encouraging.

-adv. (‘owva'rool) si guud ahaan ah. e.g. Overall, it seems to be improving. The overall situation is promising. -n. overalls, dhaaraan; surweel iyo shaar isku-tol ah oo dhar laga dul xirto. -overalled adj.

overalls

overarm (‘owvar,aarm) adj. & adv. kor-u-laacyo. overawe (,owvar'ow) v. [usu. be overawed] ka cajabin ama ka yaabsad.

overbear (,owvar'ber) v. -bearing; -bore; -borne. ku caddaadin ama ku khasbid; ku dirqin.

overbearing (,owvar'bering) adj. ku digasho iyo kibir badan. {mutajabir}. e.g. He is a very overbearing man ager. -overbearingly adv.; -overbearingness n.

overbid (,owvar'bidh) v. -bid, -bidding. sheegad qaymaha ugu sarreeya, siiba xaraash.

-n. (‘owvar,bidh) yeelasho qaymaha ugu sarreeya. -overbidder n.

overbite (‘owvar,baayt) n. isqaniinis; isdulsaaris ilkaha qalka sare iyo kan hoose.

overblown (‘owvar'balawn) adj. 1 aad u buun-buunsan. e.g. The overblown story amazed me. 2 ubax aad u buufsan ama u furan.

overboard (‘owvar,boordh) adv. qof, markab, ama doon biyo ku dhex-dhaca. e.g. The sailor fell overboard. -go overboard, aad ugu talax-tagid; aad ugu fogaan. e.g. She went overboard for him.

-throw something overboard, ku xooryo ama ku tuuryo biyo.

overbore (,ovar'boor) past of overbear.

overborne (,owvar,boorn) past participle of overbear. overburden (,owvar'bardhan) v. 1 xambaarsan ama ku raran rar culus. e.g. Refugees were overburdened with bags. 2 saarid xil ama hawl culus.

-n. dhagax ama ciid xambaarsan macdin ama khayraad kale. -overburdensome adj.

overbuy (,owvar'baay) v. -bought, -buying. gadatin in ka badan baahida.

overcame (,owvar'kam) past of overcome.

overcapacity (,owvarka'paasidhi) n. awood ka badan wax soosaarka alaab ama waxqabad hawl.

overcast (‘owvar'kaasti) adj. 1 cir leh daruuro cimir ah; cadar ah. e.g. The forecast is for overcast skies and a chilly day. 2 la xor-tolo si aysan u dun-siiban, siiba maro.

-n. (‘owvar,kaasti) cadar; daruuro buuxiya cirka. e.g. The moon was obscured by a gray cloudy overcast. -v. (,owvar'kaasti) -cast, -casting. 1 ku daboolid ama ku qarsoomid daruur ama mugdi. e.g. The small village, overcast with the shadow of the big mountain. 2 xor tolid.

overcharge (,owvar'jaarj) v. -charged, -charging. 1 saarid ama ka qaadid qamye dheeraad ah. e.g. The store over charged me for the coat. 2 siin danabayn dheeraad ah batari (battery).

overcloud (,owvar'kalowdh) v. daruuraysan; qorsoomid; haraysmid.

overcoat (‘ovar,kowt) n. jubbad dheer oo dharka laga korxirto.

 overcoat

overcome (,owvar'kam) v. -came, -come, -coming. 1 ka dulmaryo ama ka guulaysad, siiba dhibaato ama halgan. e.g. Someday we shall overcome difficulties and our own faults. 2 ka badin; ka raayn; jabin. 3 [usu. be overcome] adkaysad, siiba qiiro. e.g. He was overcome with thrill.

overconfident (,owvar'kaanfidhanti) adj. kalsooni iyo isku hallayn aad ah. -overconfidence n.; -overconfidently adv.

overcrop (,owvar'karaap) v. -cropped, -cropping. dilid ciid ayada oo joogto wax loogu abuuro.

overcrowd (,owvar'karowdh) v. buux-dhaafid [as adj.] overcrowded, buux-dhaafay. e.g. Overcrowded prisons.

overdo (,owvar'dhuu) v. -did, -done, doing. 1 samayn ama isku-dayid in badan. e.g. Don't overdo your exercise. 2 [often as adj.] overdone, dab-dhicid; bisayl-dhaafid. e.g. The rice was overdone. 3 qabatin hawl badan.
